model versioning and migration system is implemented across multiple layers:\\n\\n## Backend Schema Version Migration (Go)\\n\\n### Core Migration Infrastructure\\nThe migration system is orchestrated through `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/migrate.go` which exports the `Migrate()` function as the main entry point. The `Initialize()` function sets up the migrator singleton with required datasource provider dependencies. The migration.go file implements a comprehensive pipeline that:\\n1. Applies frontend defaults (DashboardModel constructor defaults)\\n2. Applies panel defaults (PanelModel constructor defaults)\\n3. Executes sequential schema version migrations (v0 → v42)\\n4. Cleans up the dashboard to match frontend getSaveModel behavior\\n\\n### Dashboard Schema Versions\\nThe schema versions are defined in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go` which maintains a registry of all version migrations (v2 through v42) via the `GetMigrations()` function that returns a map of version-to-migration-function mappings. Version constants MIN_VERSION (0) and LATEST_VERSION (42) are defined here, along with the SchemaVersionMigrationFunc type and DataSourceInfoProvider interface for dependency injection.\\n\\n### Field-Level Migration Functions\\nEach schema version (v2.go through v42.go) implements a specific migration function that handles field-level transformations:\\n\\n- **v2.go (V2)**: Migrates legacy services.filter structure to modern time and templating.list format\\n- **v6.go (V6)**: Moves annotations from pulldowns array to structured annotations object\\n- **v7.go (V7)**: Converts nav array to timepicker structure\\n- **v14.go (V14)**: Migrates sharedCrosshair boolean property to graphTooltip integer property\\n- **v16.go (V16)**: Complex migration that upgrades from row-based layout to modern grid-based layout, including panel ID assignment and grid position calculations\\n- **v36.go (V36)**: Migrates datasource references from legacy string format to structured UID-based objects with type and apiVersion information\\n- **v42.go (V42)**: Latest schema version\\n\\nMigration functions from v3-v5, v8-v13, v15, v17-v35, v37-v41 are no-op migrations that only update the schema version for consistency.\\n\\n### Migration Utilities\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migration_utils.go` provides shared utility functions for type-safe field extraction and conversion across all migrations:\\n- GetStringValue(), GetBoolValue(), GetIntValue(), GetFloatValue() for safe field access\\n- ConvertToFloat(), ConvertToInt() for flexible numeric type conversions supporting floats, ints, and string suffixes like \\\"700px\\\"\\n- IsArray() for type checking\\n\\n### Error Handling\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/errors.go` defines:\\n- MigrationError: Error type for migration failures with context about current version, target version, and function name\\n- MinimumVersionError: Error for dashboards below the minimum migration support version
